-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Structure de la table `VALIDE`
--

CREATE TABLE `VALIDE` (
  `SP_MATRICULE` varchar(7) NOT NULL,
  `FOR_ID` varchar(32) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`SP_MATRICULE`,`FOR_ID`),
  KEY `I_FK_VALIDE_POMPIER` (`SP_MATRICULE`),
  KEY `I_FK_VALIDE_FORMATION` (`FOR_ID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

--
-- Contraintes pour les tables exportées
--

--
-- Contraintes pour la table `EXERCER`
--
ALTER TABLE `EXERCER`
  ADD CONSTRAINT `exercer_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`SP_MATRICULE`) REFERENCES `POMPIER` (`SP_MATRICULE`),
  ADD CONSTRAINT `exercer_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`FCT_ID`) REFERENCES `FONCTION` (`FCT_ID`);

--
-- Contraintes pour la table `FORMATION`
--
ALTER TABLE `FORMATION`
  ADD CONSTRAINT `formation_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`FCT_ID`) REFERENCES `FONCTION` (`FCT_ID`);

--
-- Contraintes pour la table `INSCRIRE`
--
ALTER TABLE `INSCRIRE`
  ADD CONSTRAINT `inscrire_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`SP_MATRICULE`) REFERENCES `POMPIER` (`SP_MATRICULE`),
  ADD CONSTRAINT `inscrire_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`FOR_ID`) REFERENCES `FORMATION` (`FOR_ID`);

--
-- Contraintes pour la table `LOGIN`
--
ALTER TABLE `LOGIN`
  ADD CONSTRAINT `login_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`SP_MATRICULE`) REFERENCES `POMPIER` (`SP_MATRICULE`);

--
-- Contraintes pour la table `POMPIER`
--
ALTER TABLE `POMPIER`
  ADD CONSTRAINT `pompier_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`GRA_ID`) REFERENCES `GRADE` (`GRA_ID`),
  ADD CONSTRAINT `pompier_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`CIS_ID`) REFERENCES `CASERNE` (`CIS_ID`);

--
-- Contraintes pour la table `VALIDE`
--
ALTER TABLE `VALIDE`
  ADD CONSTRAINT `valide_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`SP_MATRICULE`) REFERENCES `POMPIER` (`SP_MATRICULE`),
  ADD CONSTRAINT `valide_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`FOR_ID`) REFERENCES `FORMATION` (`FOR_ID`);
